==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The null check is broken since it will throw a NullPointerException itself. It is likely that you used || instead of && or vice versa.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// should be &&
public class Foo {
    Object buz;
    Object bar(Object list) {
        if (list != null || !list.equals(buz)) {
            return list;
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNullCheck(node.getCondition(), new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        
        if (condition instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infix = (ASTInfixExpression) condition;
            
            if (infix.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
                JavaNode left = infix.jjtGetChild(0);
                JavaNode right = infix.jjtGetChild(1);
                
                if (left instanceof ASTVariableAccess && right instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node.getCondition(), null)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================第4轮为第一个测试用例生成checker========================
=========================logics=========================
1. Get the condition of the if statement.
        2. Check whether the condition contains a null check using || operator.
        3. Check whether the condition contains an equality check using ! operator.

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node.getCondition(), new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullChecked(condition)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(condition, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getCondition() != null && JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node.getCondition(), new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// should be &&, but now with a longer expression
class Books {
    String getJane() { return null; }
    void bar(Books books) {
        if (books.getJane()!= null || !books.getJane().equals("")) { }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 2
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2) {
            ASTExpression condition = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
            if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(condition, StablePathMatcher.QUICK)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return data;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node.getCondition(), StablePathMatcher.INSTANCE)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(condition, null) && condition.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

        If the condition of the if statement contains both null check and method invocation, then this test case violate the rule.

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        if (condition instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) condition;
            if (infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3 && infixExpression.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        if (condition instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) condition;
            if (infixExpr.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3) {
                JavaNode firstChild = infixExpr.jjtGetChild(0);
                JavaNode secondChild = infixExpr.jjtGetChild(1);
                JavaNode thirdChild = infixExpr.jjtGetChild(2);

                if (firstChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess && thirdChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess 
                    && secondChild instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        
        if (condition instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) condition;
            
            if (infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3) {
                JavaNode firstChild = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
                JavaNode secondChild = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(1);
                JavaNode thirdChild = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(2);
                
                if (firstChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess && thirdChild instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) firstChild;
                    ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) thirdChild;
                    
                    if (variableAccess.getImage().equals("null") && JavaAstUtils.isEqualsMethod(methodCall.getFullMethodName())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
// 1633683, should be ||, but now with another compare
public class Foo {
    void bar(String str) {
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        
        if (condition instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) condition;
            if (infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3) {
                ASTExpression left = (ASTExpression) infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
                ASTExpression right = (ASTExpression) infixExpression.jjtGetChild(2);
                
                if (left instanceof ASTVariableAccess && right instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) left;
                    ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) right;
                    
                    if (variableAccess.getImage().equals("str") && methodCall.getImage().equals("length")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(condition, StablePathMatcher.create("NullLiteral"))) {
            addViolation(data, condition);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTCompilationUnit.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2) {
                if (infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess && infixExpression.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getCondition() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression condition = (ASTInfixExpression) node.getCondition();
            if (isNullCheck(condition, StablePathMatcher.of(ASTNullLiteral.class, ASTLiteral.class))) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return data;
    }

        // You can implement the logic here based on the provided APIs

    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression condition = node.getCondition();
        
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(condition, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
                    result = boo == null && boo != false; // same
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetParent();
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = assignment.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getImage() != null && leftOperand.getImage().equals("result")) {
                ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
                ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
                if (leftInfix != null && rightInfix != null && leftInfix.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2 && rightInfix.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
                    JavaNode leftChild1 = leftInfix.jjtGetChild(0);
                    JavaNode leftChild2 = leftInfix.jjtGetChild(1);
                    JavaNode rightChild1 = rightInfix.jjtGetChild(0);
                    JavaNode rightChild2 = rightInfix.jjtGetChild(1);
                    
                    if (leftChild1 instanceof ASTVariableAccess && leftChild2 instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        if (rightChild1 instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightChild2 instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            Node leftOperand = node.jjtGetChild(0);
            Node rightOperand = node.jjtGetChild(1);
            
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightOperand instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            ASTExpression rightOperand = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);

            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTNullLiteral && rightOperand instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                ASTExpression leftOperand = ((ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetParent()).getLeftOperand();
                if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    if (((ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand).getVariableName().equals(((ASTNullLiteral) node.jjtGetChild(0)).getImage())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return data;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            JavaNode leftChild = (JavaNode) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            JavaNode rightChild = (JavaNode) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            
            if (leftChild instanceof ASTNullLiteral && rightChild instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
            if (rightChild instanceof ASTNullLiteral && leftChild instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression leftOperand = (ASTInfixExpression) node.getChild(0);
            ASTInfixExpression rightOperand = (ASTInfixExpression) node;
            
            if (isNullCheck(leftOperand, StablePathMatcher.DEFAULT) && isNullCheck(rightOperand, StablePathMatcher.DEFAULT)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The null check is broken since it will throw a NullPointerException itself. It is likely that you used || instead of && or vice versa.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// BrokenNullCheck with Boolean variable
class Test{
                public void testPMD(){
                    Boolean boo = null;

                    boolean result;

                    result = boo != null || boo != true;  // second expression will throw
                    result = boo != null || boo != false; // second expression will throw
                    result = boo != null || boo == true;  // second expression will throw
                    result = boo != null || boo == false; // second expression will throw

                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 4
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            Node left = node.jjtGetChild(0);
            Node right = node.jjtGetChild(1);

            if (left instanceof ASTNullLiteral && right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            } else if (right instanceof ASTNullLiteral && left instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (isNullCheck(node, StablePathMatcher.NULL_LITERAL_MATCHER)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            ASTExpression leftExpression = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            ASTExpression rightExpression = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);

            if (isNullCheck(leftExpression) && isNullCheck(rightExpression)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return data;
    }

    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTExpression expression) {
        if (expression instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) expression;
            if (infixExpression.getOperator() == ASTInfixExpression.Operator.NOT_EQUAL) {
                ASTExpression leftOperand = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
                ASTExpression rightOperand = infixExpression.getLastChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);

                if (leftOperand instanceof ASTName && rightOperand instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getLastChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && rightOperand != null && rightOperand.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTNullLiteral && rightOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() != 2) {
            return super.visit(node, data);
        }

        ASTExpression leftOperand = ((ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetParent()).getLeftOperand();
        ASTExpression rightOperand = ((ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetParent()).getRightOperand();

        if (isNullCheck(leftOperand, StablePathMatcher.thisOrParent(ASTNullLiteral.class)) &&
            isNullCheck(rightOperand, StablePathMatcher.thisOrParent(ASTNullLiteral.class))) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return data;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess).getJVariableSymbol())) {
            if (node.isBooleanOperator() && node.isAndOperator()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, null)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
// BrokenNullCheck with other kinds of NPEs (see QualifiableExpression)
class Test {
                interface FunctionalItf { String describe(); }

                public void testPMD(){

                    boolean result;

                    result = boo == null && boo.new Inner().isEmpty();       // qualified ctor call

                }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class, ASTMethodReference.class, ASTMethodCall.class, ASTFieldAccess.class, ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodReference node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFieldAccess node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTVariableDeclaratorId node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, new StablePathMatcher())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class, ASTMethodCall.class, ASTFieldAccess.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, StablePathMatcher.of(ASTNullLiteral.class))) {
            addViolation(node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, StablePathMatcher.of(ASTNullLiteral.class))) {
            addViolation(node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFieldAccess node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, StablePathMatcher.of(ASTNullLiteral.class))) {
            addViolation(node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2 && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (infixExpression.getOperator() == ASTInfixExpression.Operator.AND) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return data;
    }
}

    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() != 2) {
            return data;
        }
        
        ASTExpression left = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
        ASTExpression right = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
        
        if (isNullCheck(left) && isNullCheck(right)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        return data;
    }
    
    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTExpression expr) {
        return expr.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTEqualityExpression && expr.jjtGetParent().jjtGetNumChildren() == 2
            && expr.equals(expr.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(0));
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 1 && node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (assignment.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2 && assignment.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) assignment.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (variableAccess.jjtGetNumChildren() == 1 && variableAccess.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableDeclaratorId) {
                    ASTVariableDeclaratorId variableId = (ASTVariableDeclaratorId) variableAccess.jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (variableId.getType().equals("int[]") && assignment.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) assignment.jjtGetChild(1);
                        if (infixExpression.isAndOperator() && infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
                            ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                            if (nullLiteral != null) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            ASTExpression left = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            ASTExpression right = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            
            if (isNullCheck(left) && isNullCheck(right)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return data;
    }

    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTExpression expression) {
        if (expression instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) expression;
            ASTExpression leftOperand = infixExpression.getLeftOperand();
            ASTExpression rightOperand = infixExpression.getRightOperand();
            
            if (infixExpression.getOperator() == InfixExpression.Operator.EQUALS && rightOperand instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2 && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infix = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (infix.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2 && infix.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression innerInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) infix.jjtGetChild(1);
                if (innerInfix.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2 && innerInfix.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTArrayAccess) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 1 && node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = assignment.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getVariableName().equals("result")) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = assignment.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpression != null) {
                    ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                    if (nullLiteral != null) {
                        ASTInfixExpression innerInfixExpression = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                        if (innerInfixExpression != null) {
                            ASTArrayAccess arrayAccess = innerInfixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class);
                            if (arrayAccess != null) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            ASTExpression rightOperand = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);

            if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(leftOperand, StablePathMatcher.INSTANCE)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```java
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
```

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, StablePathMatcher.of("==", "null"))) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            JavaNode leftNode = node.jjtGetChild(0);
            JavaNode rightNode = node.jjtGetChild(1);
            
            if (leftNode instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightNode instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
                    result = i == null && i << 1;
                    result = i == null && i + 0;
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaRuleUtil.isNullCheck(node, StablePathMatcher.IDENTITY_MATCHER)) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            // Add your logic to check for broken null checks here
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
